  <script>
   function termtype()
        {
         
         if((navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i))||(navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i)))
         {
          var exdate=new Date();
          exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate()+365);
          SetCookie('termtype','iphone',exdate,'/');
         }
         else
         {
           var exdate=new Date();
           exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate()+365);
           SetCookie('termtype','none',exdate,'/');
         }
        }
        termtype();
  </script>
  <script language="JavaScript">
   var nbClick = 0;
var Mouse_Xs = 0;
var Mouse_Ys = 0;
function findPosSX(obj)
{
    var curleft = 0;
    if (obj.offsetParent)
    {
        while (obj.offsetParent)
        {
            curleft += obj.offsetLeft;
            obj = obj.offsetParent;
        }
    }
    else if (obj.x)
        curleft += obj.x;
    return curleft;
}
function findPosSY(obj)
{
    var curtop = 0;
    if (obj.offsetParent)
    {
        while (obj.offsetParent)
        {
            curtop += obj.offsetTop
            obj = obj.offsetParent;
        }
    }
    else if (obj.y)
        curtop += obj.y;
    return curtop;
}
function sendPos(posX,posY)
{
   var MyHttpLink = "/temp/Mstat.php?X="+posX+"&Y="+posY+"&type=4";
   http.open("GET", MyHttpLink, true);
   http.send(null);
}
function catchClicks(e) {
  var Mouse_X;
  var Mouse_Y;
  var Haut_Y;
  // L'événement est passée à la fonction
  // donc tous sauf IE
  if(e){                     // Dans ce cas on obtient directement la position dans la page
   Mouse_X = e.pageX;
   Mouse_Y = e.pageY;
  }
  else{                      // Dans ce cas on obtient la position relative à la fenêtre d'affichage
    Mouse_X = event.clientX;
    Mouse_Y = event.clientY;

    //-- Il faut traiter le CAS des DOCTYPE sous IE
    if( document.documentElement && document.documentElement.clientWidth) // Donc DOCTYPE
      DocRef = document.documentElement;   // Dans ce cas c'est documentElement qui est réfèrence
    else
      DocRef = document.body;                    // Dans ce cas c'est body qui est réfèrence

    
    //-- On rajoute la position liée aux ScrollBars
    Mouse_X += DocRef.scrollLeft;
    Mouse_Y += DocRef.scrollTop;
  }
 
  Mouse_X -= findPosSX(window.document.getElementById("mySITE"));
  //Mouse_Y -= findPosSY(window.document.getElementById("mySITE"));
  //Haut_Y = findPosSY(window.document.getElementById("myCENTER"));
  Haut_Y = findPosSY(window.document.getElementById("zbCenter"));
  Haut2_Y = findPosSY(window.document.getElementById("tdFvDroite"));
  
  //alert(Mouse_X+"**"+Mouse_Y+"**"+Haut_Y);
  
  if (Mouse_X==Mouse_Xs&&Mouse_Y==Mouse_Ys)
   return;
  if (Mouse_Y>0&&Mouse_Y<Haut_Y)
   return;
  if (Mouse_Y>=Haut_Y || Mouse_Y>=Haut2_Y)
  {
   if (Mouse_X>1000)
    Mouse_Y-=Haut2_Y;
   else
    Mouse_Y-=Haut_Y;
   Mouse_Y+=1;  
  }
  //alert(Mouse_X+"**"+Mouse_Y+"**"+Haut_Y);
  Mouse_Xs=Mouse_X;
  Mouse_Ys=Mouse_Y;
  nbClick++;
  sendPos(Mouse_X,Mouse_Y);     
  //window.document.getElementById("debug").innerHTML=nbClick+":"+Mouse_X+" -- "+Mouse_Y;
}

// catch clicks at the document level
document.onmousedown=catchClicks;
document.onmouseclick=catchClicks;
//document.onmouseup=catchClicks;

// if the document has layers, let the top level window catch the click events
if (document.layers) {
        window.captureEvents(Event.MOUSEDOWN);
        window.captureEvents(Event.MOUSECLICK);
       // window.captureEvents(Event.MOUSEUP);
}

// catch clicks at the window level
window.onmousedown=catchClicks;
window.onmouseclick=catchClicks;
//window.onmouseup=catchClicks;
  </script>

             $(document).ready(function() {
                //Dynamic remove overflow row
                $(function(){
                    new ResizeSensor($('#hcLeft2'), function(){ 
                        checkAndHideContent();
                    });
                    
                    checkAndHideContent();    
                });
                
                function checkAndHideContent()
                {                                 
                    if(($('#hcLeft2').height()-50)>$('#hcLeft1').height())
                    {             
                        $($('#editableDecryptages').find("a")[$('#editableDecryptages').find("a").length-1]).remove();                            
                    }        
                }
            });

            <script>
             function switch_sec_per_reg(zone)
            {
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_W').className="tabTab4";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_US').className="tabTab4";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_A').className="tabTab4";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_E').className="tabTab4";
            //
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lkW').innerHTML="World";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lkUS').innerHTML="United States";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lkA').innerHTML="Asia";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lkE').innerHTML="Europe";
            //
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lkW').className="link3";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lkUS').className="link3";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lkA').className="link3";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lkE').className="link3";
            //
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_'+zone).className="tabTabChosen4";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lk'+zone).className="link3C";
            document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lk'+zone).innerHTML="<b>"+document.getElementById('n_sec_per_lk'+zone).innerHTML+"</b>";

            $('#n_sec_per').append("<div style=\"position:absolute;top:0px;left:0px;text-align:center;background-color:#EEE;opacity:0.8;filter:alpha(opacity=80);height:100%;width:100%\"><img src=\"/images/loading_100.gif\"></div>");
            $('#n_sec_per').css('background-color', "#EEE");
            $.ajax({
                    url: '/mods_a/news/sector_performance.php',
                    type: 'get',
                    data: 'zone='+zone,
                    success: function(data) {
                      $('#n_sec_per').css('background-color', "#FFF");
                      $('#n_sec_per').html(data);
                    }
                  });
            }
            </script>

       <script language="Javascript" type="text/javascript">
        function changeIndexesTab(iTab)
    {
        var sNewStyle = "",
            chosenTabStyle = "tabTabChosenBlk",
            notChosenTabStyle = "tabTabBlk",
            chosenLinkStyle = "linkBlkC",
            notChosenLinkStyle = "linkBlk",
            header = $("#tab_indexes_"+iTab).parent().find(">table").find("."+chosenTabStyle+",."+notChosenTabStyle);
        
        //unset bold style for current chosen tab
        $("#tab_indexes_"+iTab).parent().find(">table").find(".tabTabChosen4").find("a").html($("#tab_indexes_"+iTab).parent().find(">table").find(".tabTabChosen4").find("a").text());
        for(var i = 0; i<4; i++)
        {
            sNewStyleDiv = (iTab==i) ? "" : "none";
            sNewsStyleTd = (iTab==i) ? chosenTabStyle : notChosenTabStyle;
            sNewsStyleLink = (iTab==i) ? chosenLinkStyle : notChosenLinkStyle;
            $("#tab_indexes_"+i).css('display',sNewStyleDiv);    
            $(header[i]).removeClass(chosenTabStyle+" "+notChosenTabStyle);    
            $(header[i]).addClass(sNewsStyleTd);     
            $(header[i]).find("a").removeClass(chosenLinkStyle+" "+notChosenLinkStyle);    
            $(header[i]).find("a").addClass(sNewsStyleLink);
            if(sNewsStyleLink==chosenLinkStyle)
                $(header[i]).find("a").html("<b>"+$(header[i]).find("a").text()+"</b>");
            else
                $(header[i]).find("a").html($(header[i]).find("a").text());        
        }
        return false;
    }
       </script>


    
function showGraphIndice(tab,iLine)
{
    $.each(aCodeZbIndexesHome[tab],function(i,val){                                           
        $("#graphIndice"+tab+"_"+val).css("display","none");      
    });
    
    //check if charts need to set src
    if($("#graphIndice"+tab+"_"+aCodeZbIndexesHome[tab][iLine]).prop("src").indexOf(aCodeZbImagesIndex[aCodeZbIndexesHome[tab][iLine]])==-1)
    {
        $("#graphIndice"+tab+"_"+aCodeZbIndexesHome[tab][iLine]).prop("src",aCodeZbImagesIndex[aCodeZbIndexesHome[tab][iLine]]);
    } 
        
    $("#graphIndice"+tab+"_"+aCodeZbIndexesHome[tab][iLine]).css("display","");
    
    var aTrToUpdate = $("#tab_indexes_"+tab).find("table").find("tr");
    $.each(aTrToUpdate,function(iLine,trToUpdate)
    {
        $(trToUpdate).removeClass('tr_hovered');
    });
    $(aTrToUpdate[iLine]).addClass('tr_hovered');
}

$(function()
{
    showGraphIndice(0,0); 
    showGraphIndice(1,0); 
    showGraphIndice(2,0); 
    showGraphIndice(3,0);   
    
    $.each(aCodeZbIndexesHome,function(index,aCodezb)
    {
        var aTrToUpdate = $("#tab_indexes_"+index).find("table").find("tr");
        
        $.each(aTrToUpdate,function(iLine,trToUpdate)
        {
            $(trToUpdate).mouseover(function(){
                showGraphIndice(index,iLine);   
            });
        });    
    });
});
       </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        function changePalmares(select,numPalm)
    {
        if(select.value=="not_set")
            return false;         
        var expires = new Date();
        expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (7*24*60*60*1000));
        SetCookie("lastPal"+numPalm,select.value,expires,"/","marketscreener.com");
        loadPalmares(numPalm,'');
    }
    
    function loadPalmares(numPalm,areacode)
    {
        $.ajax({
            url : "/mods_a/palmares/taballpalmares.php?bDroiteHome=1",
            context : document.body,
            async : true,
            data : {ajaxpalmares: 1, numPalm: numPalm, areacode: areacode},
            type : 'GET'
        })
        .done(function(data)
        {
            $("#content_palmares_"+numPalm).empty();
            $("#content_palmares_"+numPalm).append(data);
            
            var indexToLoad = GetCookie("lastPal"+numPalm);

            if((indexToLoad == null) || (indexToLoad == ""))
            {
                indexToLoad = (numPalm==1 ? 'index_sp500' : (numPalm==2 ? 'index_nasdaq100' : 'index_eurostoxx600'));            }
                //return;
            loadHeatmap("heatmap_"+numPalm,indexToLoad);
        });
    }
    
    function loadHeatmap(container,index)
    {                                        
        var chart = new Highcharts.Chart({
            chart : {
                style :
                {
                    fontFamily : 'Arial'
                },
                marginTop: 0,
                marginLeft: 0,
                marginRight: 0,
                marginBottom: 0,
                ignoreHiddenSeries: false,
                renderTo: container
            },

            colorAxis: {
                min: -3,
                max: 3,
                stops: [
                    [0, '#ff0000'],
                    [0.5, '#222222'],
                    [1, '#00ff00']
                ],
                endOnTick: false,
                startOnTick: false
            },

            title: {
                text: null
            },

            credits: {
                enabled: false
            },

            tooltip: {
                backgroundColor: {
                    linearGradient: {
                        x1: 0,
                        y1: 0,
                        x2: 0,
                        y2: 1
                    },
                    stops: [
                        [0, 'white'],
                        [1, '#EEE']
                    ]
                },
                borderColor: 'gray',
                borderWidth: 1,
                borderRadius: 5,
                headerFormat: "",
                pointFormatter: function(){
                    return "<table style='width: 100%;' class='highchartsTooltipTab'><tr><td colspan='2'><span style='font-size: 12px'>"+this.link+"</span></td></tr><tr><td>Size : </td><td style='text-align: right;'><b>"+Highcharts.numberFormat(Math.floor(this.size / 1000000),0)+" M$</b></td></tr><tr><td>Change : </td><td style='text-align: right;'><span style='color: "+((this.varia>0)?'#008000':'#CC0000')+";'><b>"+this.varia.toFixed(2)+"%</b></span></td></tr></table>";
                },
                style: {
                    pointerEvents: 'auto'
                },
                useHTML: true
            },

            plotOptions: {
                treemap : {
                    allowDrillToNode: false,
                    borderWidth: 1,
                    dataLabels: {
                        enabled: false,
                        allowOverlap: false
                    },
                    drillUpButton: {
                        position: { 
                            align: 'left',
                            x: 0,
                            y: 0
                        },
                        text: "< Back"
                    },  
                    layoutAlgorithm: 'squarified',
                    layoutStartingDirection: 'horizontal',     
                    levelIsConstant: true,
                    levels: [{
                        level: 1,
                        dataLabels: {
                            enabled: true,
                            style: {
                                fontSize: "10px",
                                "fontWeight": "normal"
                            }
                        },
                        borderColor: "#FFFFFF"
                    }],     
                    opacity: 1,          
                    states: {
                        hover: {
                            borderColor: '#FFEE00',
                            dataLabels: {
                                enabled: true
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            },

            legend: {
                enabled : false
            }
        });                                              
        
        chart.showLoading();
        
        $.ajax({url : '/mods_a/graph/heatmap_sector.php',
            data : {zone : index,  varia : 'F271', type: "sectors", modeDetail: 0},
            context : document.body,
            async : true,
            type : 'POST',
            success : function(data)
            { 
                var aData = [],
                    aTemp;    
                try
                {
                    aTemp = JSON.parse(data)    
                }
                catch(e)
                {
                    console.log("erreur JSON parse : "+e);
                    console.log("data received : "+data);
                    return;
                }
                
                $.each(aTemp,function(index,val)
                {
                    if(typeof val['parent'] === "undefined" || val['parent']==null)
                    {            
                        delete val['child'];
                        
                        if(typeof (val['colorValue'] === "undefined"))
                            val['colorValue'] = val['color'];
                            
                        if(typeof (val['value'] === "undefined"))
                            val['value'] = val['size'];
                        aData.push(val);                         
                    }
                });
                
                if(chart.get('myHeatmap'))
                {
                    chart.get('myHeatmap').setData(aData);
                    chart.get('myHeatmap').update({
                        levels: [{
                            level: 1,
                            dataLabels: {
                                enabled: true,
                                style: {
                                    fontSize: "10px",
                                    "fontWeight": "normal"
                                }
                            }
                        }]
                    });
                }
                else
                {
                    chart.addSeries({
                        type: "treemap",
                        id: 'myHeatmap',
                        data: aData,
                        name: "Heatmap",
                        levels: [{
                            level: 1,
                            dataLabels: {
                                enabled: true,
                                style: {
                                    fontSize: "10px",
                                    "fontWeight": "normal"
                                }
                            }
                        }]
                    });
                }

                var index = 0;

                if($("#periodeHM").val()=='F217')
                    index=1;
                else if($("#periodeHM").val()=='F218')
                    index=2;

                /*Highcharts.charts[0].colorAxis[0].update({
                    min: aSeuils[index][0],
                    max: aSeuils[index][1]
                });*/

                chart.hideLoading();
            }
        });
    }
    
    $(function(){
        $.ajaxSetup({
            cache: false
        });
        
        /*update cookies if they were previously set*/
        if(GetCookie("lastPal1"))
        {
            var expires = new Date();
            expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (7*24*60*60*1000));
            SetCookie("lastPal1",GetCookie("lastPal1"),expires,"/","marketscreener.com");
        }
        if(GetCookie("lastPal2"))
        {
            var expires = new Date();
            expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (7*24*60*60*1000));
            SetCookie("lastPal2",GetCookie("lastPal2"),expires,"/","marketscreener.com");
        }   
        if(GetCookie("lastPal3"))
        {
            var expires = new Date();
            expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (7*24*60*60*1000));
            SetCookie("lastPal3",GetCookie("lastPal3"),expires,"/","marketscreener.com");
        }             
loadPalmares(1,'');loadPalmares(2,'');loadPalmares(3,'');    });
       </script>


    
function showGraphForex(iLine)
{
    $.each(aCodeZbForexHome,function(i,val){
        $("#graphForex"+"_"+val).css("display","none");        
    });
    
    //check if charts need to set src
    if($("#graphForex"+"_"+aCodeZbForexHome[iLine]).prop("src").indexOf(aCodeZbImagesForex[aCodeZbForexHome[iLine]])==-1)
    {
        $("#graphForex"+"_"+aCodeZbForexHome[iLine]).prop("src",aCodeZbImagesForex[aCodeZbForexHome[iLine]]);
    } 
    
    $("#graphForex"+"_"+aCodeZbForexHome[iLine]).css("display","");
    
    var aTrToUpdate = $("#tab_Forex").find("table").find("tr");
    $.each(aTrToUpdate,function(iLine,trToUpdate)
    {
        $(trToUpdate).removeClass('tr_hovered');
    });
    $(aTrToUpdate[iLine]).addClass('tr_hovered');
}

$(function()
{
    showGraphForex(0); 
    
    $.each(aCodeZbForexHome,function(index,aCodezb)
    {
        var aTrToUpdate = $("#tab_Forex").find("table").find("tr");
        
        $.each(aTrToUpdate,function(iLine,trToUpdate)
        {
            $(trToUpdate).mouseover(function(){
                showGraphForex(iLine);   
            });
        });    
    });
});

       <script>
        function sticky_relocate() {
    var window_top = $(window).scrollTop();
    var div_top = $('#sticky-Left1-anchor').offset().top;
    if (window_top > div_top) {
        $('#sticky-Left1').addClass('stick');
        $('#sticky-Left1-anchor').height($('#sticky-Left1').outerHeight());
    } else {
        $('#sticky-Left1').removeClass('stick');
        $('#sticky-Left1-anchor').height(0);
    }
}

$(function() {
    $(window).scroll(sticky_relocate);
    sticky_relocate();
});
       </script>

  <script>
   var aViewableDiv = [];
      var aViewedDiv = [];
      function inArray(needle, haystack) {
            var length = haystack.length;
            for(var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                if(haystack[i] == needle) return true;
            }
            return false;
      }
      function ksort(w) 
      { 
          var sArr = []; 
          var tArr = []; 
          var n = 0; 
          for (i in w) 
          { 
            tArr[n++] = i; 
          } 
          //tri du plus petit au plus grand 
          tArr = tArr.sort(function(a, b) {
              if (a == b)
               return 0;
              else 
               return (a<b ? 1 : -1)
          }); 
          n = tArr.length; 
          for (var i=0; i<n; i++) { 
            sArr[tArr[i]] = w[tArr[i]]; 
          } 
          return sArr; 
      }
       
      var socket;
      function startStreaming()
      {
       socket = io('https://live.zonebourse.com:8157',{
          reconnection: false,
      });
      socket.on('status', function (data) {
        socket.emit('auth', { hkKey: "5ecaa6951d6aa5abdd9c84d0591c2f8f", pvKey: "4f135648f91a48c7f783205cfc537087", uKey:"Lw==" });
      });
      socket.on('auth_confirm', function (data) {
                ZBLiveDLY();
        if (typeof ZBLiveDLY_droite === "function") { 
         ZBLiveDLY_droite();
        }
        else {
         setTimeout(function(){ if (typeof ZBLiveDLY_droite === "function") { ZBLiveDLY_droite(); }},15000);
        }
                
        $( window ).scroll(function() {
            var docViewTop = $(window).scrollTop();
            var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $(window).height();
           
            for (i=0;aViewableDiv.length>i;i++)
            {
              if (jQuery.inArray(aViewableDiv[i],aViewedDiv)!=-1) {
                continue;
              }
                
              var elemTop = $("#tab_"+aViewableDiv[i]).offset().top;
                
              if ((elemTop <= docViewBottom)) {
                aViewedDiv.push(aViewableDiv[i]);
                window["ZBLiveDLY_"+aViewableDiv[i]]();
              }
            }
        });  
      });
      socket.on('event', function (type,data)
      { 
              if (type=="QUOTES")
       {
        data.ID_NOTATION     = data.I;
        data.PRICE           = data.C;
        data.HIGH            = data.H;
        data.LOW             = data.L;
        data.BID             = data.B;
        data.ASK             = data.A;
        data.PERFORMANCE_PCT = data.P;
        data.DATETIME_PRICE  = data.DC;
        data.DATETIME_BID  = data.DB;
        data.DATETIME_ASK  = data.DA;

                if (Array.isArray(ZBL_notation) && Array.isArray(ZBL_notation[data.ID_NOTATION]))
        {
         ZBL_notation[data.ID_NOTATION].forEach(function(element) {
             if (element=='fv')
              ZBL_priceFV(data,false);
             else if (element=='fv2')
              ZBL_priceFV2(data);
             else if (element=='fv3')
              ZBL_priceFV(data,true);
             else if (element=='fv4')
              ZBL_priceFV(data,true,true);
             else if (element=='multi' || element=='multi2' || element.substring(0,6)=='multi3')
              ZBL_Mutli(data,element);
         }); 
        }
       }
       else if (type=="MS_QUOTES")
       {
        data.ID_MORNINGSTAR  = data.id;
        data.BID             = data.B;
        data.ASK             = data.A;
        data.DATETIME_BID  = data.DB;
        data.DATETIME_ASK  = data.DA;

        if (Array.isArray(ZBL_MScode) && Array.isArray(ZBL_MScode[data.ID_MORNINGSTAR]))
        {
         ZBL_MScode[data.ID_MORNINGSTAR].forEach(function(element) {
            if (element=='fv2')
              ZBL_priceFV2(data);
            else if (element=='multiMS' || element=='multiMS2')
              ZBL_Mutli(data,element);
         }); 
        }
       }
       else if (type=="MSCI_QUOTES")
       {
        data.ID  = data.id;
        data.PRICE = data.P; 
        data.DATETIME_PRICE = data.T;

        if (Array.isArray(ZBL_MSCIcode ) && Array.isArray(ZBL_MSCIcode [data.id]))
        {
         ZBL_MSCIcode [data.id].forEach(function(element) {
            if (element=='fv2')
              ZBL_priceFV(data,true);
         }); 
        }
       }
       else if (type=="TTM_QUOTES")
       {
        data.PRICE = parseFloat(data.P).toFixed(2);
        data.DATETIME_PRICE = data.T;
        
        if (Array.isArray(ZBL_TTMcode) && Array.isArray(ZBL_TTMcode[data.id]))
        {
         ZBL_TTMcode[data.id].forEach(function(element) {
             if (element=='fv2')
              ZBL_priceFV(data,true);
             else if (element=='fv4')
              ZBL_priceFV(data,true,true);
             else if (element=='multi' || element=='multi2' || element.substring(0,6)=='multi3')
              ZBL_Mutli(data,element,"ttmzero");
         });
        }
       }
       else if (type=="NEWS")
       {
         if (data.myElement.substring(0,4)=="FRM_")
           ZBL_forum(data.myElement,data.sMessage);
         else
           ZBL_update(data.myElement,data.sMessage);
       }
              });
            }

   function gaEvent(eventCategory, eventAction, eventLabel, eventValue)
        {
                      if (typeof eventValue !== 'undefined')
              ga('send', 'event', eventCategory, eventAction, eventLabel, eventValue);
             else if (typeof eventLabel !== 'undefined')
              ga('send', 'event', eventCategory, eventAction, eventLabel);
             else
              ga('send', 'event', eventCategory, eventAction);
                     }
        function gaTiming(timingCategory, timingVar, timingValue)
        {
                       ga('send', 'timing', timingCategory, timingVar, timingValue);
                     }
        function gaSocial(socialNetwork, socialAction, socialTarget)
        {
                     ga('send', 'social', socialNetwork, socialAction, socialTarget);
                    }
        function gaPageview(page_path)
        {
                       ga('send', 'pageview', page_path);
                     }
